String.prototype.gblen = function() {
    var len = 0;
    for (var i=0; i<this.length; i++) {
        if (this.charCodeAt(i)>127 || this.charCodeAt(i)==94) {
            len += 2;
        } else {
            len ++;
        }
    }
    return len;
}

    var len = 0;
    for (var i=0; i<this.length; i++) {
        if (this.charCodeAt(i)>127 || this.charCodeAt(i)==94) {
